Examples

certificate > generate

Request:

<packet>
  <certificate>
    <generate>
      <info>
        <bits>2048</bits>
        <country>RU</country>
        <state>NSO</state>
        <location>Novosibirsk</location>
        <company>Parallels</company>
        <email>info@example.com</email>
        <name>example.com</name>
      </info>
    </generate>
  </certificate>
</packet>

Response:

customer > add

Request:

<packet>
  <customer>
    <add>
      <gen_info>
        <pname>John Smith</pname>
        <login>john-unit-test</login>
        <passwd>simple-password</passwd>
      </gen_info>
    </add>
  </customer>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <customer>
    <add>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <id>86</id>
        <guid>a72218f8-849c-46a8-a026-9c19ddd59994</guid>
      </result>
    </add>
  </customer>
</packet>

customer > del

Request:

<packet>
  <customer>
    <del>
      <filter>
        <id>86</id>
      </filter>
    </del>
  </customer>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <customer>
    <del>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <filter-id>86</filter-id>
        <id>86</id>
      </result>
    </del>
  </customer>
</packet>

customer > del (2)

Request:

<packet>
  <customer>
    <del>
      <filter>
        <login>customer-a</login>
      </filter>
    </del>
  </customer>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <customer>
    <del>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <filter-id>customer-a</filter-id>
        <id>89</id>
      </result>
    </del>
  </customer>
</packet>

customer > get

Request:

<packet>
  <customer>
    <get>
      <filter>
        <id>88</id>
      </filter>
      <dataset>
        <gen_info/>
      </dataset>
    </get>
  </customer>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <customer>
    <get>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <filter-id>88</filter-id>
        <id>88</id>
        <data>
          <gen_info>
            <cr_date>2016-11-11</cr_date>
            <cname/>
            <pname>John Smith</pname>
            <login>john-unit-test</login>
            <status>0</status>
            <phone/>
            <fax/>
            <email/>
            <address/>
            <city/>
            <state/>
            <pcode/>
            <country/>
            <locale>en-US</locale>
            <guid>07e12e15-4ecc-488b-a9bf-675e61fc9a07</guid>
            <owner-login>admin</owner-login>
            <vendor-guid>bec05900-a696-11e6-bf5c-0242ac110002</vendor-guid>
            <external-id/>
            <description/>
            <password>$5$/e2C5Wfurhtsh8Zc$4WOkIqk4oP0tGfrSmLferCtG/vcAqhhtaKljiBJBhB7</password>
            <password_type>crypt</password_type>
          </gen_info>
        </data>
      </result>
    </get>
  </customer>
</packet>

customer > get (2)

Request:

<packet>
  <customer>
    <get>
      <filter/>
      <dataset>
        <gen_info/>
      </dataset>
    </get>
  </customer>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <customer>
    <get>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <filter-id>89</filter-id>
        <id>89</id>

            <status>0</status>
            <phone/>
            <fax/>
            <email/>
            <address/>

            <pcode/>
            <country/>
            <locale>en-US</locale>
            <guid>452594d0-c802-455c-9ed0-24bd4c8da75d</guid>
            <owner-login>admin</owner-login>
            <vendor-guid>bec05900-a696-11e6-bf5c-0242ac110002</vendor-guid>
            <external-id/>
            <description/>
            <password>$5$jgo1EC09qYwdSX1y$Pb0nU3AZl6v0LA/CknQPTwmlu4bP7TxQvjjkWyEkf67</password>
            <password_type>crypt</password_type>
          </gen_info>
        </data>
      </result>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <filter-id>90</filter-id>
        <id>90</id>
        <data>
          <gen_info>
            <cr_date>2016-11-11</cr_date>

            <external-id/>
            <description/>
            <password>$5$8m/V9biuG7olp3cK$rT9qdaL9gfzKUMcfozGYCn0k8qJJrGcQljPAZLm26m1</password>
            <password_type>crypt</password_type>
          </gen_info>
        </data>
      </result>
    </get>
  </customer>
</packet>

db_server > get-supported-types

Request:

<packet>
  <db_server>
    <get-supported-types/>
  </db_server>
</packet>

Response:

<packet version="1.6.8.0">
  <db_server>
    <get-supported-types>
      <result>
        <status>ok</status>
        <type>mysql</type>
        <type>postgresql</type>
      </result>
    </get-supported-types>
  </db_server>
</packet>

<packet>
  <event_log>
